Welcome Everyone

Join us in service to our community through our events, and initiati= ves. Our motto is "friend of youth". We supply scholarships through essa= y competitions, we support our community with food-drives, and help kids with anxiety issues learn coping sk= ills through our initiative with M.I. Understanding. Wether you attend our events or join our club this is a rewarding e= xperience, and a great way to give back to the community.
